line=1017 tag=M+AC:       Chronicle for 1137, c.1154
line=1018 tag=L:       I ne can ne i ne mai tellen all þe
line=1019 tag=L:       wunder ne alle þe pines ð hi diden wreccemen on þis land. 7 ð laste-
line=1020 tag=L:       de þa .xix. wintre wile Stephne was king 7 æure it was uuerse 7
line=1021 tag=L:       uuerse.
line=1022 tag=L:       þa was corn dære. 7 flec 7 cæse 7 butere. for nan ne wæs o þe land.
line=1023 tag=L:       Wreccemen sturuen of hungær.
line=1024 tag=L:       war sæ me tilede, þe erthe ne bar nan corn. for þe land was al
line=1025 tag=L:       fordon. mid suilce dædes. 7 hi sæden openlice ð crist slep 7 his ha-
line=1026 tag=L:       lechen. Suilc 7 mare þanne we cunnen sæin. we þolenden .xix. wintre
line=1027 tag=L+AC:       for ure sinnes (from facsimile edition of the Peterborough Chronicle,
line=1028 tag=L+AC:       D. Whitelock (ed.), Copenhagen: Rosenkilde & Bagger, 1954).
line=1029 tag=B:
line=1030 tag=M+LN:       Version in West Saxon Old English
line=1031 tag=B:
line=1032 tag=L+AL:       ic ne cann ne ic mæg tellan ealle þa
line=1033 tag=L+AL:       wundor ne ealle þa pinas þe hie dydon wreccum mannum on þissum lande. 7 þæt
line=1034 tag=L+AL:       læste-de þa .xix. wintra þa hwile þe Stephne cyning wæs 7 æfre hit wæs wyrsa 7
line=1035 tag=L+AL:       wyrsa.
line=1036 tag=L+AL:       þa wæs corn deore. 7 flesc 7 cese 7 butere. for nan ne wæs on þæm lande.
line=1037 tag=L+AL:       wrecce menn sturfon of hungre.
line=1038 tag=L+AL:       swa hwær swa man tilode. seo eorþe ne bær nan corn. for þæt land wæs eall
line=1039 tag=L+AL:       fordon. mid swilcum dædum. 7 hie sædon openlice þæt crist slep 7 his ha-
line=1040 tag=L+AL:       lgan. swilc 7 mare þanne we cunnon secgan. we þolodon .xix. wintra
line=1041 tag=L+AL:       for ure synna.
line=1042 tag=B:
line=1043 tag=M:       Translation
line=1044 tag=B:
line=1045 tag=G:       I ne can ne I ne may tell all the
line=1046 tag=G:       horrors ne all the pains that they caused wretched-men in this land. & that last-
line=1047 tag=G:       ed the 19 winters while Stephen was king & ever it was worse & worse.
line=1048 tag=G:       then was corn dear. & flesh & cheese & butter. for none ne was in the land.
line=1049 tag=G:       Wretched-men died of hunger.
line=1050 tag=G:       where so one tilled. the earth ne bore no corn. for the land was all
line=1051 tag=G:       ruined. with such deeds. & they said openly that christ slept & his saints.
line=1052 tag=G:       Such & more than we can say. we suffered 19 winters
line=1053 tag=G+AC:       for our sins (from Freeborn 1992: 49).
